PitBull - huge optimization change.
Now when the raid changes, instead of updating every unit, instead switch around the data on the frames themselves so that in the end, only 1 member (the new one) will need to have an update call, potentially down from 40.
- added module method :OnSwapUnitFrame("unit", frame, oldFrame)
- added module method :OnUnitFrameUnitChange("unit", frame, "lastUnit")
PitBull_Portrait - update to use :OnUnitFrameUnitChange.
Note: this commit needs to be tested thoroughly, specifically in raids and battlegrounds.

r408 | roartindon | 2007-04-04 01:40:43 +0000 (Wed, 04 Apr 2007) | 9 lines
Changed paths:
   M /tmp/trunk/PitBull/CastBar/CastBar.lua
   M /tmp/trunk/PitBull/Layouts/ABF.lua

PitBull:

- CastBars could magically disappear before. If combat is initiated with a ranged attack (eg. Fireball) and a 2nd cast occurs relatively quickly after, then the game could send a UNIT_SPELLCAST_START before it sends the in-combat event (PLAYER_REGEN_DISABLED). The Combat code would create a combat icon, then call a relayout of frames. The relayout of frames called ABF.lua's castBar layout which hid the in-progress castbar!

Fix is in 2 parts

- 1. Commented out the castBar:Hide() call in ABF.lua. This unfortunately exposes a different problem - the castbar shows up full while until a unit casts something (when it's meant to be hidden).
2. CastBar.lua - the initial castbar is set to zero alpha

------------------------------------------------------------------------
